</th>

<span class="expandline" title="20 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_viola&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the viola</a></span>; <th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>Version History
<ul><li> Composed for string sextet, 1859–60
</li><li> Arranged for piano 4 hands by Brahms, ca.1861.
</li><li> The second movement was arranged by Brahms in 1860 for solo piano as an independent work entitled <a href="/wiki/Theme_and_Variations,_Op.18b_(Brahms,_Johannes)" title="Theme and Variations, Op.18b (Brahms, Johannes)">Theme and Variations</a> in D minor
</li></ul>
</td></tr></table>
</div>
